              }</style><script>function getCookie(name) {
                  const value = `; ${document.cookie}`;
                  const parts = value.split(`; ${name}=`);
                  if (parts.length === 2) return parts.pop().split(';').shift();
              }
  
              function getQueryParam(name) {
                  const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
                  return urlParams.get(name);
              }
  
              function setCookie(name, value, domain, path, secure, sameSite, expirationDays) {
                  if (getCookie(name)) return;
  
                  const expirationDate = new Date();
                  expirationDate.setDate(expirationDate.getDate() + expirationDays);
                  
                  document.cookie = `${name}=${value}; Domain=${domain}; path=${path}; ${secure ? 'secure;' : ''} SameSite=${sameSite}; expires=${expirationDate.toUTCString()};`;
              }
  
              const utmTargetValue = getQueryParam('utm_target');
              if (utmTargetValue) {
                  setCookie('utm_target', utmTargetValue, '.minerent.net', '/', true, 'Strict', 30);
              }

                  { keyword: 'eloy', value: 'eloy' },
                  { keyword: 'topor7', value: 'topor7' },
              ];
